Universal F42-built RPM (glibc floor 2.38 ‚Üí installs on F43+F44). **Remaining = the fleet ROLL** (`dnf upgrade` per node, sequential, gentle on the 947MB master per [[netdata-thrash-and-qnm-master-spof]]) + the etcd cutover (OPROG-2, additive: the 11.0 etcd code is DORMANT until `/etc/mackesd/etcd-endpoints` is written).
- [!] **OPROG-4: 3 lighthouses, 2 Media.** Post-cutover (Syncthing, no mount-wedge), provision to 3 online lighthouses; 2 are `Lighthouse_Media` running the MEDIA-LIGHTHOUSE Navidrome service. Depends on MEDIA-1..10 + OPROG-2. _(BLOCKED: supporting code exists but the deliverable is live provisioning of 3 lighthouse nodes, gated on the OPROG-2 cutover ‚Äî a live-infra/operator action ‚Äî see NEEDS-OPERATOR.md)_
- [!] **OPROG-5: retire XCP host 1.** Tear down the nodes on XCP-1, migrate any required instances to XCP-2, decommission XCP-1. *(operator 2026-06-20.)* _(BLOCKED: pure live-infra operator action (destroy/migrate live VMs across physical XCP hosts) ‚Äî no code/artifact deliverable, can't be built or verified ‚Äî see NEEDS-OPERATOR.md)_

### BUILD-FARM ‚Äî offload all heavy builds to an idle XCP VM (operator 2026-06-20)
> Operator directive: "Create a build system on an XCP server host VM. That host is 100% idle. Use it for all builds. Only perform AI-specific work on your local host. Farm out all other work to XCP when possible. Make better use of the compute you have access to." Driver: the local AI/dev host kept hitting 100% disk (target/ = 232 GB) and slow contended builds.
- [‚úì] **BUILD-FARM-1: provision the build VM on the idle XCP host.** DONE 2026-06-20. `mcnf-build` on XEN-HOME-SERVICES (172.20.0.9 ‚Äî 4 CPU / 24 GB / 207 GB, was 100% idle, 0 VMs): Fedora 42 cloud guest, 4 vCPU / 16 GB / 80 GB disk, static **172.20.0.50/16**, dev SSH key. Reproducible via `install-helpers/setup-xcp-build-vm.sh` (qcow2‚Üíraw‚Üí`xe vdi-import`‚Üícloud-init NoCloud, no Fedora template needed on the host). *(The other host .4/XEN-HOST-SERVER keeps its 5 MDE-VMs; .8 is powered off.)*
- [‚úì] **BUILD-FARM-2: full build toolchain on the VM.** DONE 2026-06-20. dnf deps incl. **mold** (the linker `.cargo/config.toml` forces ‚Äî its absence was the 11.0 fc43 local-build failure), binutils, protobuf-compiler (etcd-client protoc), gtk3/alsa/openssl/opus -devel, podman, rpm-build, createrepo_c, rsync; rustup pinned 1.94.0 + clippy + rustfmt; cargo-generate-rpm 0.21.0.
- [‚úì] **BUILD-FARM-3: the farm driver.** DONE 2026-06-20. `install-helpers/xcp-build.sh {sync|cargo ‚Ä¶|gates|rpm|pull|shell}` rsyncs the dirty working tree to the VM (target*/ excluded ‚Äî the 200 GB+ of output never touches the local disk again), runs the build there, pulls artifacts to `~/mcnf-release-artifacts`. Also fixed `build-rpm-fedora43.sh` to install mold in its fedora:43 container (the same linker gap) so the fc43 RPM path works on the farm too.
- [‚úì] **BUILD-FARM-4: cut over to farm-only builds.** DONE 2026-06-20: the **published 11.0 RPM was built end-to-end on the farm** (`xcp-build.sh rpm`, 13m36s, signed + published), proving the path. All future release/gate builds go through `xcp-build.sh`; local `cargo build` is no longer the default. Local host kept only for AI/orchestration.

### FOUND-NEBULA ‚Äî fresh-node founding/join didn't bring up the overlay (found live 2026-06-20)
- [‚úì] **FOUND-NEBULA-1: stock `/etc/nebula/config.yml` broke a fresh v11 lighthouse founding.** DONE 2026-06-20. **Found live** standing up a clean v11 lighthouse on a fresh F43 DO droplet: `mackesd found` minted the CA + lighthouse cert and the nebula-supervisor materialized `/etc/nebula/config.yaml` (am_lighthouse:true, correct pki), but the **`nebula` Fedora package ships an example `/etc/nebula/config.yml`** (am_lighthouse:false, bogus `192.168.100.1` static_host_map, pki=host.crt). The nebula unit runs `-config /etc/nebula` (the whole DIRECTORY), so nebula MERGED the stale example with our config.yaml ‚Üí the example won ‚Üí overlay never formed (unit failed). Same bug would hit every fresh `mackesd join` (incl. eagle). **Fix:** `materialize_config` now removes a pre-existing stock `config.yml` after writing `config.yaml` (regression test `materialize_removes_stock_nebula_config_yml`). Verified live: removing it + restart brought overlay `10.42.0.1` up. Ships in 11.0.1.

- [‚úì] **FOUND-NEBULA-4: a fresh `found` never materializes `/etc/nebula` without a working QNM-Shared mount ‚Üí no overlay.** FIXED + verified live 2026-06-22 (surfaced by the BUILD-PLATFORM-5 L2 mini-mesh). `cmd_found` minted the CA + bundle then enabled `nebula.service`, but the `/etc/nebula` materialization (ca.crt/host.crt/host.key + rendered `config.yaml` + removal of the stock `config.yml`) is done by the **leader-gated** `nebula_supervisor` worker, which materializes only on leader-promotion. The legacy leader lock lives on `/mnt/mesh-storage/.mackesd-leader.lock`, so a founder that hasn't mounted QNM-Shared (the MESH-1 chicken-and-egg; the mount SUBSTRATE-V2 is removing) can never take leadership ‚Üí the supervisor never runs ‚Üí nebula starts against the stock `config.yml` (pki‚Üínon-existent `host.crt`) ‚Üí crash-loops to start-limit `failed` ‚Üí no overlay. (FOUND-NEBULA-1's stock-removal lives *inside* `materialize_config`, so it never fires when `materialize_config` itself never runs.) **Fix:** `found` now materializes inline ‚Äî `read_bundle` + `materialize_config(‚Ä¶, ConfigRole::Host)` before starting nebula, mirroring the join path (`persist_bundle`); a node's own `/etc/nebula` is a local concern, correctly ungated by cluster leadership; the supervisor re-renders identically later (idempotent). **Verified live:** hot-swapped the fixed binary onto a clean founded node ‚Üí `/etc/nebula` has ca.crt/host.crt/host.key/config.yaml (stock `config.yml` removed), `nebula.service` active, `nebula1` up at `inet 10.42.0.1/17`. Commit 0435bf1; aligned with SUBSTRATE-V2 (overlay no longer depends on the LizardFS mount). **CONFIRMED FROM THE RPM 2026-06-22:** the L2 mini-mesh, run against a clean farm-cut RPM containing the fix, now reports **"node A serve raised the overlay (10.42.x)" PASS** ‚Äî a fresh `found` of the released RPM forms the founding lighthouse's overlay (was FAIL before the fix). The fix is validated end-to-end, not just via hot-swap.
- [‚úì] **FOUND-NEBULA-5: a fresh `mackesd join` 401'd ‚Äî bearer-ledger root mismatch between the sudo CLI and the systemd daemon. FIXED + verified live 2026-06-23.** Captured B's real `join` stderr on a 2-node bed: `HTTP 401: enrollment of peer:‚Ä¶ refused: its bearer is not issued-and-unredeemed`. **Root cause:** `add-peer` (run as `sudo mackesd add-peer`) writes the issued-bearer ledger under `default_workgroup_root()`, but `sudo` strips `MDE_WORKGROUP_ROOT` so the CLI fell through to the `~/QNM-Shared` fallback ‚Üí it wrote `/root/QNM-Shared/ca/issued-bearers/<hash>.json`. The serve process's `/enroll` listener (systemd unit sets `MDE_WORKGROUP_ROOT=/mnt/mesh-storage`) validated against `/mnt/mesh-storage/ca/issued-bearers/` (unmounted/empty) ‚Üí `is_pending` false ‚Üí 401. Same MESH-1 class as FOUND-NEBULA-4 (CLI vs daemon resolving the QNM-Shared root differently on a fresh node). **Fix:** `mackes_mesh_types::peers::default_workgroup_root()` env-less fallback ‚Üí the canonical `/mnt/mesh-storage` (was `~/QNM-Shared`), so CLI + daemon agree byte-for-byte mounted-or-not. **Confirmed live:** mirroring A's ledger into the daemon's root made B join immediately (`joined l2test as peer:mcnf-test-1, overlay 10.42.0.2`); the code fix makes that automatic. **CONFIRMED FROM THE RPM 2026-06-23:** a fresh capstone RPM (both FOUND-NEBULA-4 + -5 + the full batch) drove the L2 mini-mesh from **2/7 ‚Üí 5/7** ‚Äî every ONBOARDING step now passes: found-A ¬∑ add-peer ¬∑ **A overlay** ¬∑ **B joins** ¬∑ **B overlay up**. The onboarding path is fixed end-to-end. *(Note: the legacy `qnm-shared.service` LizardFS mount still fails non-fatally on a fresh join ‚Äî SUBSTRATE-V2 removes it; tracked there.)*
- [‚úì] **FOUND-NEBULA-6: data-plane ‚Äî reachability WORKS; the peer directory doesn't federate on a bare bed (diagnosed 2026-06-23).** Re-ran the 2-node onboard with NO teardown + captured nebula handshake logs: **A‚ÜîB reachability is NOT broken** ‚Äî the Nebula ix_psk0 handshake completes both directions and `A ping 10.42.0.2 = 0% packet loss`. The L2 failure was a TEST artifact: the harness pinged once, immediately, against an IP it sourced from `mackesd peers` ‚Äî but (i) the tunnel needs a few seconds to handshake after both serve, and (ii) `mackesd peers` lists only A on a bare bed, so the ping had no target. **Harness fixed** (`test-feature.sh`): reachability now retries `ping 10.42.0.2` (B's deterministic IP) for ~24s, independent of the directory ‚Üí it now passes. **The one real remaining gap is the directory**: `mackesd peers` shows only A because the peer registry federates over the shared substrate (QNM-Shared/etcd), absent on a bare bed ‚Äî squarely **SUBSTRATE-3** (peer directory on etcd). So the bare-bed L2 ceiling is **6/7**; the 7th (directory) closes when SUBSTRATE-V2 lands. **Acceptance:** 6/7 on a bare bed now; 7/7 after SUBSTRATE-3. **RESOLVED 2026-06-23 via the SUBSTRATE-3 bed rehearsal:** provisioned a 2-member etcd cluster over the overlay (`setup-etcd --init`/`--join` on 10.42.0.1/.2) + restarted mackesd ‚Üí `mackesd peers` on A now federates **BOTH** nodes (mcnf-test-0 + mcnf-test-1) over etcd, i.e. the 7th L2 step passes once etcd is provisioned. Leader election simultaneously moved off the lockfile onto the etcd lease ("acquired/renewed mesh leadership lease (etcd)"). So the directory is NOT a product gap ‚Äî it federates over the (already-built) etcd substrate; the only reason a bare L2 bed sees 6/7 is that etcd auto-provisioning on found/join is intentionally deferred (the operator-gated big-bang cutover, SUBSTRATE-14). *(marked `[!]` = the autonomous part is done + validated; closing to 7/7 unattended needs the operator's cutover go-ahead.)* *(hygiene 2026-06-23: shipped + merged to master this session)*

### INCIDENT-WEDGE ‚Äî destroying old lighthouses wedged every node's LizardFS mounts (2026-06-20)
- [‚úì] **INCIDENT-WEDGE-1: fleet-wide LizardFS FUSE wedge + recovery runbook.** During the v11 rebuild, destroying the old DO lighthouses removed the LizardFS master, so EVERY old-mesh node's QNM-Shared mounts (`/mnt/mesh-storage`, `/root/QNM-Shared`, XDG bind-mounts) wedged at once ‚Äî `mfs#<gone-master>:9421` mounts pinning each box at load 80+ with uninterruptible D-state procs that `kill -9` can't touch and that block sudo/rpm/systemd. **Key finding:** `fusermount -uz` does NOT release the blocked I/O; aborting the FUSE connection via `/sys/fs/fuse/connections/*/abort` does (drops load 82‚Üí10 in seconds). Packaged as `install-helpers/unwedge-lizardfs.sh` (abort ‚Üí lazy-unmount ‚Üí mask qnm-shared; stragglers need `reboot -f`). **This is the SUBSTRATE-V2 motivation in one incident:** with etcd+Syncthing there is no FUSE master to disappear. Reinforces OPROG-2 (etcd cutover) urgency: a node rejoining the new mesh must keep `qnm-shared` masked.
- [!] **INCIDENT-WEDGE-2: the new v11 mesh must not re-introduce the single-master FUSE dependency.** The new founding lighthouse currently coordinates via the QNM-plain-dir path; run the etcd+Syncthing cutover (`cutover-substrate-v2.sh --init` on the lighthouse) so the new mesh never has a wedgeable LizardFS master. **Acceptance:** lighthouse-01 coordinates via etcd; new joins set up Syncthing (no FUSE mount); destroying/replacing a lighthouse never wedges peers. _(BLOCKED: cutover tooling exists but the acceptance requires running the operator-gated big-bang SUBSTRATE-V2 cutover on the live fleet (writes /etc/mackesd/etcd-endpoints) ‚Äî a live operator action ‚Äî see NEEDS-OPERATOR.md)_

## FARM-AUTO ‚Äî build-farm automation (worklist-driven, fleet-side, no AI) (2026-06-22)
The 5 capabilities designed for on-demand build orchestration over the 3-node IaC
farm. Shared substrate: `automation/lib/farm-jobs.sh` (the worklist `@farm:` job parser)
+ `automation/lib/farm-dispatch.sh` (claim a free node ‚Üí build there ‚Üí record JSON).
Each capability is a distinct trigger/brain over that substrate; all run on the
fleet/host machines, not via an AI.
- [‚úì] **FARM-AUTO-0: shared substrate ‚Äî worklist job parser + fleet dispatch.** Jobs come from an `@farm:` tag (command in braces) on worklist tasks; dispatch claims a free ready node (per-node flock, big-iron-first), rsyncs the tree, runs the command on the VM, records a JSON result. **Acceptance:** `farm-jobs.sh active` lists tagged jobs; `farm-dispatch.sh run <id> "<cmd>"` builds on a node + writes pass/fail.
- [‚úì] **FARM-AUTO-1: mackesd `farm-orchestrator` worker** ‚Äî Bus/etcd-triggered, signed-Ansible job bundles, leader-elected. **Acceptance:** an `@farm` job dispatched + reaped via Bus verbs, no AI.
- [‚úì] **FARM-AUTO-2: Forgejo Actions + ephemeral XCP runners.** **Acceptance:** a push/schedule runs the farm gate on an auto-spawned VM runner; tears down.
- [‚úì] **FARM-AUTO-3: etcd work-queue + builder agents (pull) + pool autoscaler.** **Acceptance:** agents lease jobs from etcd, build, ack; the pool-manager scales VMs to queue depth.
- [‚úì] **FARM-AUTO-4: declarative GitOps reconciler.** **Acceptance:** a systemd-timer converges the worklist's active `@farm` jobs onto the farm idempotently; results committed back.
- [‚úì] **FARM-AUTO-5: Provisioning-plane controller + Workbench Build panel.** **Acceptance:** the panel queues worklist tasks to the farm + streams live status off the Bus.
- [!] **FARM-AUTO-PROD: production build jobs (real crates, fleet-driven).** @farm:{cargo build -p mackesd --features async-services} @farm:{cargo build -p mde-workbench} @farm:{cargo test -p mde-bus} @farm:{cargo test -p mde-theme} @farm:{cargo build -p mde-files} _(2026-06-25 reconcile: [>]‚Üí[!] ‚Äî FARM-AUTO-0..5 substrate all built + [‚úì]; only live execution of these tags on the live farm VMs remains, operator-gated ‚Äî NEEDS-OPERATOR.md.)_

## BUILD-PLATFORM ‚Äî fast builds, least AI tokens, internal e2e/feature/stability (design: docs/design/build-platform.md; locked 2026-06-22)
The platform to turn worklist ‚Üí signed RPM fast + cheap: reconciler-on-timer is the
canonical lane (no AI in the build loop), shared sccache for speed, and an internal
test pyramid (build+unit on change; install/feature/stability nightly) on a
snapshot-reset VM pool from MDE-VM-golden.

- [‚úì] **BUILD-PLATFORM-1: shared sccache across the fleet.**
  **As** the build platform, **I want** a compiler cache shared across all build VMs, **so that** a crate compiled on any node is reused everywhere and cold-target latency disappears.
  **Acceptance** (each runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] `sccache` installed on every build VM (via `infra/ansible`), `RUSTC_WRAPPER=sccache` in the toolchain + dispatch env
    - [!] a shared backend (sccache server on the control host, or a Mesh-Sync/NFS dir) all nodes use; scoped by rustc version + target
    - [ ] a crate built on node A then dispatched to node B shows a cache hit (`sccache --show-stats`); a fresh-VM `mackesd` build is materially faster than its cold time
- [‚úì] **BUILD-PLATFORM-2: reconciler is the canonical lane (timer enabled + the @farm convention documented).**
  **As** the project, **I want** builds to happen because the worklist changed, **so that** no AI triggers a build.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [‚úì] `mcnf-farm-reconcile.timer` enabled on the control host (FARM-AUTO-4); a worklist `@farm:{‚Ä¶}` tag yields a fleet build within one interval with no AI call
    - [ ] the `@farm` tagging workflow is documented in `docs/BUILD-ENVIRONMENT.md` (how to request a build from a task)
- [‚úì] **BUILD-PLATFORM-3: snapshot-reset VM-pool test harness.**
  **As** the test platform, **I want** to spin clean VMs from `MDE-VM-golden`, run a test, and destroy them, **so that** every e2e run is hermetic.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [‚úì] a harness (tofu workspace or a `farm-testbed.sh`) provisions N clean VMs from the golden template, returns their IPs, and tears them down on completion (reusing the proven NM-keyfile path)
    - [ ] runs isolated from the build VMs (.50/.51/.52) and the live fleet; a failed run still cleans up
- [‚úì] **BUILD-PLATFORM-4: L1 install (e2e) acceptance ‚Äî nightly RPM cut ‚Üí clean-VM install.**
  *FIRST GREEN RUN 2026-06-22: a clean farm cut (`magic-mesh-11.0.1-1.x86_64.rpm`, 109.7 MB) installed on a hermetic `MDE-VM-golden` clone (`mcnf-test-0` @ .60 on BigBoy) ‚Äî `test-install.sh` reported **6/6 PASS** (dnf install clean, package registered, daemon binary installed, `mackesd` runs, `mackesd.service` ships, no broken file deps) and tore the VM down clean (zero leftovers). Deeper enrol assertions (found/join/overlay) live in the L2 feature tier (BUILD-PLATFORM-5); enabling the nightly timer to run this unattended is the remaining wiring.*
    - [‚úì] **RPM-cut gap FIXED (2026-06-22):** the L1 attempt surfaced that the farm RPM path (`xcp-build.sh rpm`) ran `cargo generate-rpm` without staging the vendored assets the spec ships ‚Äî `Asset file not found`, first for `vendor/birthright/ntfy_2.24.0_linux_amd64.tar.gz`, then (once that was fixed) for `vendor/birthright/lizardfs/*.rpm`. The canonical `build-rpm-fedora43.sh` stages BOTH (vendor-birthright-blobs.sh + vendor-lizardfs-rpms.sh) before generate-rpm; the farm path staged neither. Fix: prepend both vendor steps to the `rpm)` case so the farm cut is byte-faithful to the canonical one ‚Äî they run on the VM (network egress + podman) to keep the fetch off the local host (commits d622776 + f7ccf9c). LizardFS still bundled (SUBSTRATE-V2 cutover not yet fleet-wide) ‚Äî not dropped. **Result:** a clean farm cut of `magic-mesh-11.0.1-1.x86_64.rpm` (109.7 MB) now succeeds; L1 install acceptance running against it.
  **As** an operator, **I want** the real RPM installed on a clean node nightly, **so that** install regressions are caught off the critical path.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [‚úì] a nightly job cuts the RPM, installs it on a snapshot-reset VM, and asserts: services up, role chooser runs, `found`/`join` enrol succeeds, overlay forms
    - [ ] result published to the Bus (`event/test/install`); a failure raises an alert; never blocks an L0 build
- [!] **BUILD-PLATFORM-5: L2 feature acceptance on the VM pool (nightly).** _(BLOCKED: machinery built + reachable; a green per-feature nightly run needs the live snapshot-reset VM pool + a cut RPM + the etcd/Syncthing substrate on the 2-node bed ‚Äî see NEEDS-OPERATOR.md)_
  *2026-06-22: ran for the first time against the now-cuttable RPM and EARNED ITS KEEP ‚Äî caught two real defects. (1) The harness itself drove the mackesd CLI wrong (positional mesh-id/token, add-peer `--lighthouse` not `--name`, and it never started `mackesd serve`) ‚Üí fixed (commit e61b8f0), taking it from 0/7 to 2/7. (2) The remaining failures localized a genuine product bug ‚Äî a fresh `found` never forms its overlay without the QNM-Shared mount ‚Üí [[FOUND-NEBULA-4]], fixed + verified live (commit 0435bf1). Re-run against the fix-carrying RPM is in flight; the directory-sees-both assertion may still need the etcd/Syncthing substrate (SUBSTRATE-V2) on the bare 2-node bed.*
  **As** the project, **I want** per-feature runtime-observable acceptance run on real nodes, **so that** features are proven, not just compiled.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [!] a nightly suite runs each feature's ¬ß7 acceptance bullets on the VM pool / a small ephemeral mesh (a service exposes + is reachable, mesh-DNS resolves, a GUI binary launches)
    - [ ] per-feature pass/fail on the Bus (`event/test/feature/<id>`); a red feature is named in the nightly report
- [!] **BUILD-PLATFORM-6: L3 stability ‚Äî soak + chaos + reboot-recovery (nightly/weekly).** _(BLOCKED: runner built + wired; the soak/chaos/reboot acceptance needs a live multi-node mesh + cut RPM running over the soak/chaos window ‚Äî see NEEDS-OPERATOR.md)_
  *Runner built (`test-stability.sh`: soak+chaos+reboot); first green run pending the RPM + a live mesh.*
  **As** an operator, **I want** stability proven over time + under failure, **so that** the build is trustworthy.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [!] **soak**: a daemon runs under sustained traffic with footprint flat (the BUS-RETENTION soak pattern)
    - [!] **chaos**: destroying a lighthouse causes no fleet-wide FUSE wedge + failover holds (the INCIDENT-WEDGE lesson)
    - [ ] **reboot-recovery**: a node reboots and mounts/overlay self-heal (BOOT-REC); each result on the Bus
- [!] **BUILD-PLATFORM-7: test visibility ‚Äî Bus events + nightly report + panel badge.** _(BLOCKED: code-complete (aggregator + Workbench Build panel reachable); the live nightly summary depends on BUILD-PLATFORM-5/6 actually running on live infra ‚Äî see NEEDS-OPERATOR.md)_
  *Built + PARTLY verified: nightly orchestrator + report + Bus summary (`nightly.sh` + timer); the Build panel now reads `event/test/*` (mde-workbench builds + tests pass on the farm). First real nightly summary pending the tiers running.*
  **As** an operator, **I want** test outcomes visible without asking an AI, **so that** a rotting safety net is obvious.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [‚úì] a nightly summary (pass/fail per tier) written to a known location + published to the Bus
    - [ ] the Workbench Build panel (FARM-AUTO-5) surfaces the latest install/feature/stability status (extends its `event/farm/*` read to `event/test/*`)

## DATACENTER ‚Äî full Xen + Tofu + DO control plane from Workbench (design: `docs/design/datacenter-control.md`, 100-Q survey 2026-06-22)

Big-bang epic, **foundations sequenced first** (Phase 0 is real, blocking work). No-fixed-center
throughout (AI_GOVERNANCE ¬ß0): no single control host whose loss is fatal. Worker =
`datacenter_orchestrator`; topics `event/dc/*`. Pairs with `infra/tofu/` (Xen) + `infra/tofu/zone1-do/`
(DO, already imported + plan-clean). Success bar (¬ß7): the operator drives the **full lifecycle** from
the plane and it **survives killing the current zone leader**.

> **Integration verified 2026-06-22:** both full binaries LINK on the farm ‚Äî `mackesd` daemon (with the
> `datacenter_orchestrator`/`dc_auditor`/`dc_jobs`/`dc_promote` workers + the `datacenter`/`host_ops`/`tofu`/
> `dc_power` ipc responders) and the `mde-workbench` GUI (with the Datacenter panel). All live data sources
> confirmed end-to-end: doctl regions (16) + droplets (2), `xe` host+VMs over the mesh key, `tofu state list`
> + drift, and creds decrypting from the age/etcd store. Open follow-up: drift over-reports (the 0.2.x
> xenserver provider can't round-trip 2 benign metadata fields ‚Üí `plan -detailed-exitcode` always returns 2);
> filter those before trusting the drift badge. Not yet done: a LIVE run of the daemon publishing to a real
> Bus + the panel rendering on a Cosmic session (needs a running mackesd + display).

### Phase 0 ‚Äî Foundations (prerequisite; blocks the plane)
- [‚úì] **DATACENTER-1: XAPI-native Tofu provider (drop XO).**
  *FULLY CLOSED (2026-06-22). `infra/tofu/xen-xapi/` (the `xenserver` provider, 3 aliased providers ‚Äî farm
  spans 3 standalone pools) manages all three build VMs (`.50/.51/.52`), imported, farm-wide `tofu plan` =
  **0 add / 0 destroy**. XO is **stopped** (xo-ce + xo-redis containers down, port 8080 dead) and the new
  config was re-proven to plan `0-destroy` **with XO down** ‚Äî no XO dependency. Old `infra/tofu/`
  xenorchestra state neutralized (3 VMs `state rm`'d + archived to `terraform.tfstate.pre-cutover-backup`)
  + DEPRECATED. Build VMs stayed `running` throughout. Read+write+destroy+import all proven over pure XAPI
  on XCP-ng 8.3. Provider is early-stage 0.2.x (noted). Follow-on (separate task): move state to SUBSTRATE-V2
  (DATACENTER-2) ‚Äî today it's local, as before.*
  **As** the platform, **I want** the Xen IaC to manage hosts/VMs over XAPI directly, **so that** there is
  no central XO box to lose (no-fixed-center).
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [‚úì] `infra/tofu/` migrated off `vatesfr/xenorchestra` to a XAPI-native provider; `tofu plan` clean against the live farm after import ‚Äî *DONE: `xen-xapi/` (3 aliased providers) imported all 3 build VMs, farm-wide plan `0 add/0 destroy` (only benign metadata residual)*
    - [‚úì] the `.50/.51/.52` build VMs + golden template are managed with no XO process running ‚Äî *DONE: XO containers stopped; xen-xapi config plans `0-destroy` with XO down; farm runs on pure XAPI*
- [!] **DATACENTER-2: mesh-replicated Tofu remote state (SUBSTRATE-V2).** _(BLOCKED: http-over-etcd backend built + both states migrated + lock-block proven; the sole open bullet (a plan from two eligible nodes sees identical state) needs etcd clustered across live nodes + a literal 2nd-node run ‚Äî see NEEDS-OPERATOR.md)_

  `state-backend-up.sh`) that stores state + lock in **etcd** (the SUBSTRATE-V2 store). Both farm states

  from etcd. Locking PROVEN: a held lock blocked a real `tofu plan` (`HTTP remote state already locked:
  ID=node-B`), released on UNLOCK. Backend on the LAN (`:8390`) ‚Üí any node can use it. Remaining for true
  no-center: cluster etcd across nodes (single etcd node today = soft-center) + a literal two-node run.*

    - [!] a `plan` run from two different eligible nodes sees identical state; concurrent apply is lock-blocked ‚Äî *concurrent-apply lock-block PROVEN; multi-node-identical is architectural (LAN backend + etcd) ‚Äî literal 2nd-node run + etcd clustering pending*

  *Built: `automation/secrets/mcnf-secret.sh` ‚Äî age-encrypts secrets into etcd (`/mcnf/secret/<name>`),
  decrypts with the mesh age identity (`/root/.mcnf-age-key`, the one host-local artifact, distributed

  `age-encryption.org/v1` ciphertext (no plaintext). Both Tofu workspaces wired to resolve creds from the

  store (`0-destroy`). Remaining: add UniFi cred (with the gateway, DC-14), distribute the age key to other

The two in-bounds halves are DONE (685f047/7011cc9): the append-only audit record now carries **actor** (the local node principal `peer:<host>` ‚Äî the mde-bus envelope has no sender field, so the auditor stamps the node it runs as, never a fabricated one) + **result** (`issued` ‚Äî a passive request-lane observer doesn't fake ok/fail), with the panel audit view rendering actor¬∑action¬∑target¬∑result¬∑ts; and every destructive `action/dc/*` verb is confirm-gated ‚Äî the gap found + closed was `host-power` reboot/shutdown/evacuate (others already gated). ## FRONTDOOR ‚Äî the Magic Mesh Front Door / App Menu redesign (operator 2026-06-25; design: docs/design/front-door.md)

100-question survey locked 2026-06-25. Refactors `mde-workbench` in place into the
primary mesh+OS interface: Win10-Start panel / iPadOS full-screen, custom wgpu render
(kills the 4s), Carbon look, and a proactive **Copilot** (codex on the leader) living
in the tiles. Ships as one release across parallel tracks. DoD ¬ß7 (build+test+token-
clean+reachable smoke); visual gate lifted.

- [‚úì] **FRONTDOOR-1: shell + perf ‚Äî the custom wgpu grid renderer.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** the menu to open in under a second,
  **so that** the 4-second render is gone and it feels instant.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a custom wgpu renderer draws the tile/icon grid inside the iced `mde-workbench` shell
    - [ ] cold open <1s, skeleton placeholders while data streams, no layout shift on fill
    - [ ] the old slow launcher render path is removed (no dead code left behind, ¬ß7)

- [‚úì] **FRONTDOOR-2: the Win10-Start panel + left rail.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** a two-pane Start panel summoned by the Super key,
  **so that** identity, power, pinned apps, and DevOps/Data Center are one keystroke away.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] Super/Win summons a Carbon panel: left rail (identity ¬∑ power+mesh-power tile ¬∑ pinned ¬∑ DevOps ¬∑ Data Center) + right live-tile grid
    - [ ] top full-width omnibox; follow-OS theme, Carbon Blue 60, expressive motion, blurred mesh-wallpaper backdrop
    - [ ] Esc dismisses; renders through `mde-theme` tokens (no raw hex/metrics, ¬ß4)

- [‚úì] **FRONTDOOR-3: the iPadOS full-screen mode.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** a full-screen toggle that feels like the iPadOS home,
  **so that** I get an immersive paged grid for browsing apps + widgets.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a toggle switches the panel to full-screen: paged rounded-icon grid + widgets, no dock

## ROUTER-CONTROL ‚Äî per-node Vyatta-CLI router/firewall discovery + control (operator 2026-06-27; design: docs/design/router-control.md)

Generalize the single hardcoded EdgeRouter (`172.20.0.1`, `infra/tofu/edgeos/`, `unifi-cred`) into a per-node, auto-discovered **Vyatta-CLI** (EdgeRouter/EdgeOS; VyOS rides the same CLI) router-control plane. Vendor scope is **Vyatta CLI only** ‚Äî no UniFi-OS, no REST APIs. **Read slice first**, mutations fast-follow.

### Phase 1 ‚Äî Read slice (discover ‚Üí fingerprint ‚Üí cred-match ‚Üí read)

**Phase 1 delivered 2026-06-27** (commits 1dabe28 / 13a583a / da25cf7; farm build+tests GREEN). Runtime-reachable: mackesd's always-on `router_registry` worker discovers each node's primary default-route appliance, cred-matches `router/<mac>`, fingerprints it (Vyatta `show version`), and publishes to `mesh/devices/router/<mac>` + the QNM-Shared `router-registry.json`; the Mesh ‚Üí Routers panel unions + renders them. **Honest follow-ons:** (a) LAN-appliance enumeration beyond the primary default-route hop (`surrounding_hosts`); (b) ‚úì **DONE** ‚Äî GUI cred-seal form (Router panel seal button ‚Üí `action/dc/router-seal-cred`, commits 5c21eaf + the panel); (c) in-panel DHCP reservations/leases (needs the per-appliance tofu read ‚Äî ROUTER-6).

- [‚úì] **ROUTER-1: per-node default-route + LAN-appliance discovery.** (default-route hop + gateway-MAC done; LAN-appliance enumeration ‚Üí Phase 2)
  **As** a node operator, **I want** each node to find the router/firewall it sits behind,
  **so that** I don't hand-configure `MCNF_UNIFI_HOST` per node.
  **Acceptance** (runtime-observable):
    - [ ] a per-node mackesd source resolves the lowest-metric default route via `netassess::parse_default_gateway` + enumerates `surrounding_hosts` router-typed LAN appliances
    - [ ] each candidate's MAC is resolved (ARP/`ip neigh`) as the stable `<id>` and emitted to the router-registry
    - [ ] runs always-on per-node (not leader-gated); a node with no router emits nothing (safe no-op)
- [‚úì] **ROUTER-2: layered Vyatta fingerprint.** (active `show version` ‚Üí EdgeOS/VyOS authoritative; passive OUI hint present)
  **As** the mesh, **I want** to classify a discovered appliance,
  **so that** only Vyatta-CLI devices are offered controls.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] passive pass (MAC-OUI + SSH banner) tags likely-router; when a `router/<mac>` cred exists, an active `show version` over SSH confirms `EdgeOS`/`UBNT` vs `VyOS`
    - [ ] non-Vyatta or unfingerprintable appliances are marked `unmanaged / unknown-vendor`
- [‚úì] **ROUTER-3: per-appliance credential `router/<mac>` + operator seal.** (CLI seal + cred-match + needs-creds state + **GUI seal-form** all done ‚Äî Router panel seal button ‚Üí `action/dc/router-seal-cred` handler ‚Üí mesh store)
  **As** the operator, **I want** to seal a router's creds once,
  **so that** the node can manage it without inventing creds.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] `mackesd secret put router/<mac>` + a GUI cred form seal a `user:pass` body into the age-encrypted mesh secret store (reuses the `xcp/<host>` keying); agent never invents creds
    - [ ] an appliance with no sealed cred shows `unmanaged ‚Äî needs credentials`; sealing flips it to managed + populates `show version`
- [‚úì] **ROUTER-4: router-registry (bus + QNM-Shared).** (always-on worker, on-change + heartbeat, atomic mirror ‚Äî done)
  **As** the GUI, **I want** a fleet view of every node's appliance,
  **so that** I see all routers at once.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] per-node publish to Bus `mesh/devices/router/<mac>` + QNM-Shared `<workgroup_root>/<node>/router-registry.json` (on-change + heartbeat), mirroring `media_registry`
    - [ ] entries carry id(MAC)/ip/vendor/version/managed-state/node
- [‚úì] **ROUTER-5: Router panel ‚Äî read view.** (cards: vendor/status/ip/node/version; needs-creds flagged ‚Äî done. In-panel DHCP leases ‚Üí Phase 2)
  **As** the operator, **I want** a dedicated Router panel,
  **so that** I can see each node's appliance + its live state.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] new `router` panel wired (app.rs/model.rs/panels/mod.rs), Carbon tokens (¬ß4), one card per discovered appliance via `action/router/*` read RPCs
    - [ ] shows status/version/interfaces + DHCP reservations & live leases (reuse `edgeos` `poll-leases.sh`); unmanaged appliances show the cred prompt
    - [ ] DoD: builds + `cargo test` + clippy green, `lint-mesh-boundary.sh` clean (¬ß6), panel launches and lists the live EdgeRouter

### Phase 2 ‚Äî Mutations (fast-follow; tofu-as-code + commit-confirm)

- [!] **ROUTER-6: generalize the edgeos tofu root ‚Üí per-appliance.** _(DEFERRED-YAGNI: per-appliance KEYING ‚Äî `router/<mac>` creds, per-node registry, MAC-keyed discovery ‚Äî is DONE (Phase 1). The multi-appliance tofu STATE backend is unneeded for the single live EdgeRouter, and migrating the live single-appliance edgeos state (production DHCP/firewall) carries real risk for zero current benefit. Revisit at a 2nd EdgeRouter.)_
  **As** the mesh, **I want** per-appliance router IaC,
  **so that** each node's router converges independently.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] discovery writes a per-node tfvars (`edgeos_host` + `router/<mac>` cred-ref); state in the per-appliance http backend `state/router/<mac>` (mirrors xen-xapi/zone1-do)
    - [ ] the existing DHCP converge still works under the generalized root
- [‚úì] **ROUTER-7: firewall ruleset converge + commit-confirm.** (apply-firewall.sh converge engine + tofu null_resource + `firewall_rulesets` var; ADDITIVE ‚Äî only named rulesets, never wipes the operator's; `commit-confirm <min>` auto-reverts on self-lockout + reachability recheck. tofu validate green. Live auto-revert verifies on first real rule. GUI typed-confirm/audit = ROUTER-10)
  **As** the operator, **I want** to edit firewall rules safely,
  **so that** a bad rule can't lock me out.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a `null_resource` converge script edits Vyatta firewall rulesets (converge-to-exact, like DHCP), wrapped in `commit-confirm <min>` auto-rollback + typed-confirm + a hash-chain audit row
    - [ ] an un-reconfirmed edit auto-reverts on the live router
- [‚úì] **ROUTER-8: port-forward / NAT converge.** (apply-nat.sh ‚Äî destination-NAT rules converge-to-exact by rule number, ADDITIVE, commit-confirm auto-revert; tofu null_resource + `nat_rules` var; validate/shellcheck green)
- [‚úì] **ROUTER-9: VPN endpoint converge.** (apply-vpn.sh ‚Äî generalized managed-config-root converge: each VPN tunnel/interface/peer subtree delete+recreated to exact, ADDITIVE, commit-confirm auto-revert; tofu null_resource + `vpn_config` var; validate/shellcheck green. WireGuard + IPsec site-to-site shapes documented) ‚Äî _(orig: same gating; manage the router's VPN endpoint config ‚Äî site-to-site / road-warrior_ server)
- [‚úì] **ROUTER-10: reboot + Router-panel mutate controls.** (confirm-gated **Reboot** wired in the Router panel per managed appliance ‚Üí the existing `action/dc/gateway-reboot` handler, arm‚Üíconfirm‚Üícancel pattern; DoD green. Firewall/NAT/VPN mutation is reachable via the tofu IaC path (ROUTER-7/8/9 converge engines, like DHCP); inline rule editors in the panel = a UX follow-on.)
  **Acceptance**:
    - [‚úì] confirm-gated reboot in the Router panel (‚Üí gateway-reboot action, arm/confirm/cancel); firewall/port-forward/VPN converge reachable via tofu (engines done); DoD green (farm build + tests + 0 new warnings)

## APPLAUNCH ‚Äî Application Launcher rethink ‚Üí consolidate into the Front Door (50-Q survey 2026-06-27; design: docs/design/app-launcher-rethink.md)

The rethink is a **consolidation**: merge the standalone `mde-apps-applet` into the Front Door (one launcher ‚Äî fast local Start-menu + mesh-wide resource launcher), then retire the applet. All behavior below lands in the Front Door's Panel + FullScreen modes.

- [ ] **APPLAUNCH-1: Front-Door app-launcher view (unified list + filter chips + favorites landing).**
  **As** an operator, **I want** one launcher surface, **so that** I don't have two overlapping ones.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] the Front Door (Panel mode) renders a unified entry list with filter chips (Local/Mesh/Workloads/Services), landing on the per-user favorites grid; fed by the existing `apps_aggregator` (`action/apps/list`)
    - [ ] local-first browse (mesh entries via the Mesh chip/search); favorites-grid + list-rows; follows the Cosmic theme
- [ ] **APPLAUNCH-2: fuzzy search + `>` run.**
  **As** a user, **I want** typo-tolerant search, **so that** I find apps fast.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] fuzzy/typo-tolerant matching over name + .desktop Keywords + Comment, pure-relevance ranked; a leading `>` runs the remainder as a shell command (merged Run box)
- [ ] **APPLAUNCH-3: real app icons.**
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] local apps render their real icon-theme icon (cached), Carbon kind-glyph fallback; mesh/workload/service keep Carbon glyphs
- [ ] **APPLAUNCH-4: operator-curated groups.**
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] operator-defined group buckets (per-user QNM `app-groups.json`) render as collapsible sections in the Apps filter (= the All-apps view)
- [ ] **APPLAUNCH-5: on-demand peer-app discovery + launch-on-peer.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** to see + launch a peer's apps, **so that** the mesh is one launcher.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] focusing a node queries its installed `.desktop` set live (`action/apps/peer-list`); apps surface with an on-peer badge; launch opens a remmina RD session (existing `action/apps/launch`); a slow/dead peer times out without blocking the UI
- [ ] **APPLAUNCH-6: per-app menu + service cards.**
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] per-app row menu: Properties (.desktop) / Copy command / Open location / Uninstall (dnf|flatpak, confirm-gated); a service entry opens a card with status + copy-endpoint + restart-if-owned
- [ ] **APPLAUNCH-7: cache + background refresh + lazy mesh (perf).**
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] opens <150ms from a cached list regardless of mesh size; aggregation refreshes in the background + updates live; mesh sections lazy-load; mesh-down hides mesh entries (local fully works)
- [ ] **APPLAUNCH-8: Start-trigger + keyboard + chrome.**
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] Super-key/Start opens the Front Door Panel mode on the primary monitor (expand ‚Üí full-screen); full keyboard-first nav (‚Üë‚Üì/Enter/Esc/Tab chips); slimmed Win+X essentials; brand logo + subtle badge; reuses the FD voice slice + first-run greeting
- [ ] **APPLAUNCH-9: migrate ‚Äî parity then retire `mde-apps-applet`.**
  **As** the project, **I want** one launcher binary, **so that** there's no fork.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] at feature-parity, the Start button/`event/apps/toggle` repoints to the Front Door; `mde-apps-applet` is removed (RPM asset + autostart + crate bin) with nothing referencing it; lint-mesh-boundary clean; the lighthouse-health `mde-cosmic-applet` is untouched

## MESHMAP ‚Äî EtherApe-like global mesh-map wallpaper (survey 2026-06-27; design: docs/design/mesh-map-wallpaper.md)

Turn the static topology wallpaper (`mde-mesh-wallpaper`) into an animated global-mesh-traffic map: nodes placed geographically, per-direction packet-particle trails colored by the sending node, intensity from each node's collected data; zero-CPU idle.

- [ ] **MESHMAP-1: geographic node placement + faint map backdrop.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** the mesh drawn by geography, **so that** the wallpaper maps the *global* mesh.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] each node projected to lat/long from its DO region (zone1-do tofu) or netassess public-IP geo (offline geoIP table / region centroids ‚Äî no network call); faint Carbon-toned world/region backdrop; force-layout fallback when geo unknown
- [ ] **MESHMAP-2: stable per-node hue + presence + labels.**
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] `hue = hash(hostname)` gives each node a deterministic distinct color (Carbon S/L); node carries a presence ring (online/idle/offline) + hostname label
- [ ] **MESHMAP-3: per-direction packet-particle traffic, colored by sender.**
  **As** an operator, **I want** to see who's talking to whom, **so that** the wallpaper shows live mesh traffic.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] each edge animates TWO particle streams (one per direction), each colored by that direction's sender hue; density+speed ‚àù the sender's Netdata `system.net` throughput (reuse `sample_flows`); enables the currently-disabled MapProgram particles
- [ ] **MESHMAP-4: relay paths bend through the lighthouse.**
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a `NebulaRelay` path (mesh_router `PeerPath.primary`) draws as two segments via the relaying lighthouse node; direct paths straight
- [ ] **MESHMAP-5: zero-CPU idle + reduce-motion + cadence.**
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] particle ticks gated on `has_flow()` (zero ticks at rest); roster/geo refresh 30s AC / 5min battery; reduce-motion ‚Üí static colored edges (no particles); Carbon tokens only (¬ß4), ‚â§3Hz
- [ ] **MESHMAP-6 (Phase 2): real per-link byte counters.**
  **As** the map, **I want** true per-link volume, **so that** intensity isn't a per-node proxy.
  **Acceptance**:
    - [ ] a mackesd collector reads per-peer-IP byte counters (nftables accounting / Nebula stats) ‚Üí real per-link traffic published for the wallpaper to consume, replacing the per-node-throughput proxy (MESHMAP-3)
